          <i>
           Jul 28:
          </i>
          <b>
           Best. Muscle Mansion Week. Ever.
          </b>
          The remaining worker bees of Muscle Mansion 2009 are all fast asleep right now 
(except me), after what has been the most productive week in our collective history. Between HerBiceps and FemFlex, more than 
50 different models came through our doors as both crews worked virtually non-stop every day we were here. FemFlex fans are 
sure to be happy with the great talent we had the opportunity to work with, including the two best physiques in the show - 
overall champion,
          <b>
           Angela Salvagno
          </b>
          , and light-heavyweight runner-up,
          <b>
           Christine Sabo
          </b>
          .  Among the other great 
bodybuilders we shot were Tracy Bodner, Kris Clark, Kira Neuman, Andrea Thiel, Jill Theobald, Kimm Winn, Lisa Cross, Sherri Enos, Kat Connors, 
Laurie Larson, Nicole Berg, Margaret Negrete, Lyndsay DeJager, Gabe Nicander, Bettina Kadet, Lisa Moordigian, Rebekka Armstrong, and Amanda 
Folstad (please forgive any omissions).  We also shot some terrific fitness/figure women that we know you'll love, including 
Akane Nigro-Ismeal, Jen &amp; Cindi, Marnie Holley, Laura Bailey, LaVonda Ezelle, Parilee, Gloria Keplinger, Jeanne Nimmer, and 
Taylor Waldrop (please forgive any omissions). Thanks to all the models who came out and made this week so terrific.
          <br/>
          A special thanks to our generous sponsors at UnrealMuscle.com for their financial support in producing this great event again 
this year.
          <br/>
          None of this would've been possible without our hard-working photographers,
          <b>
           Jeff Binns
          </b>
          and
          <b>
           Maryann Glascock
          </b>
          , who worked 
tirelessly to produce high-quality results for hours on end.  While it was our first time working in the field together, 
we operated as a well-oiled machine and flat-out got the job done. Fatigue and hunger never once caused us to miss work.
          <br/>
          And lastly, the most special thanks of all to my little girl, Morgan, whom I miss more than words could possibly express. 
The sound of her voice has kept Daddy going every day and I couldn't have done a thing without her. I miss you so much, 
sweetheart, and I'll see you tonite.
          <br/>

the end of the tunnel, it's going to take just short of forever to catch up on everything I owe you here. On the positive side, I've learned a 
lot of dos and don'ts for a possible overhaul of FemFlex...but don't know whether I have the patience to endure another major site 
(re)development. I'll keep you posted.

          <b>
           What's been going on at FemFlex? Where are the juicy updates we were promised??
          </b>
          I haven't been able to maintain my usual 
workflow lately due to a couple of non-FemFlex items that have been monopolizing my time recently. For those of you who are customers at 
HerBicepsCam, we've recently done a major upgrade of the security protocol and attempted to make the change as seamless as possible...but that 
has meant time away from my duties here.  Mike and I have another brand-new site that's in the final revision and testing phases now, so 
we expect it to be open within 2-4 weeks.  All I can say about it now is that you are going to LOVE this new site and what it represents for the 
future.
          <br/>
          <b>
           In
          </b>
          other news, 'Calf King'
          <a href="http://www.clips4sale.com/studio/12222">
           <b>
            Rick Dobbins
           </b>
          </a>
          and I have teamed up on a brand-new member 
site that promises to be THE favorite site of leg fans all over the world. The design and layout are complete and the content management system 
is being loaded onto our server as we speak.  We've expect 2-3 weeks of testing and if we're lucky, we'll have the billing integrated within 3 
weeks as well, so we're anticipating opening just after November 1st.
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.killercrushes.com">
           <b>
            KillerCrushes
           </b>
          </a>
          , the new wrestling site, is scheduled to launch in about a month from now.
          <br/>
          <b>
           Lastly
          </b>
          , I'm getting lots of inquiries about
          <a href="http://www.physiquedreams.com">
           <b>
            PhysiqueDreams
           </b>
          </a>
          . This is another joint project 
by Mike and me, but we're several months away from being ready to launch. In the meantime, we invite you to visit us on
          <a href="http://www.youtube.com/physiquedreams">

          </a>
          and we may even offer a few downloads for purchase before we open the member site 
next year.

          <b>
           FemSport 2008
          </b>
          is now in the books. Promoter Nancy Lockington did a tremendous job in giving me a dream 
come true - a totally outdoor event. The weather gave us an early scare, but once the rain moved on, the crew and competitors 
got down to the business of executing one of the best events I've ever seen. FemFlex is already onboard with a sponsorship pledge 
for 2009, so I'm really excited about what the next year will bring in the growth of this great event.  Way to go, Nancy - you're the tops.

          <i>
           Aug 01:
          </i>
          Jeff and I are back home now after a week at the
          <b>
           5th Annual Muscle Mansion
          </b>
          in Las Vegas. Sponsored by the 
guys at
          <a href="http://www.unrealmuscle.com/forum/index.php">
           Unreal Muscle
          </a>
          , this was our biggest and best MM yet.  Although 
I do not have a comprehensive list in front of me at this time, we had a solid week of shooting.  I was generally impressed with our 
numbers and our model selection, as always, was top shelf.  I'm disappointed that we missed out on the 3rd-place lightweight, but 
we got everyone else on our wish list from the bodybuilding competition.  Our figure numbers are smaller than usual, but we just had 
less access to them, I'm afraid.  There were a number of house-related issues that put me behind schedule from Day One, but thankfully, 
Mike, Rick, Jeff, and Sean were there to pick up the slack for me.  Thanks also to Ibby who handled the stills on the
          <b>
           Christine Sabo
          </b>
          shoot 
for us.  We also managed to do some work for a new site project that should be open within the next year, so be on the lookout for that. *wink* 
Thanks to everyone for your patience with the lack of updates this past week - prepare for a flood in the coming days.
